<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чум.html>чума́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čumá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чум.html>чумы́</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>plague, pestilence</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">specifically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the plague, the Black Death</li></ol>

***чумазый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чумазый.html>чума́зый</a> (16827)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чу-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ču-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (unclear) + the root of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мазать.html>ма́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mázatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to soil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чумазый.html>чума́зый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čumázyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)чума́зее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)чума́зей</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dirty, stained</li></ol>

***чур.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чур.html>чур</a> (18470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чур.html>чур</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čur</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in spells</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> avaunt, away
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чур.html>чур</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čur</b> menjá!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">keep away from me!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">children's talk, expresses leadership, claim to be the first</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> bags (it)! (British), dibs
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чур.html>чур</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвый</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čur</b> ja pérvyj!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">bags, I go first!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> expresses a condition</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mind you, but mind
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чур.html>чур</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:молчать.html>молча́ть</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tólʹko <b>čur</b> molčátʹ!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">but not a word, mind you!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
Related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">kiáuras</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">саũrs</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">kiùrstu, kiuraũ, kiùrti</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">skiaurė̃</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">schore</i>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>чу́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čúrka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чурка.html>чу́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чурка.html>чу́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чурка.html>чу́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>chock, block of wood</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыжий.html>чу́рка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čúrka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чурка.html>чу́рки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чурка.html>чу́рки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чурка.html>чу́рок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a dumb, uneducated person, a dullard, a booby</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">offensive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ethnic slur</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an immigrant from Central Asia or the Caucasus, a wog</li></ol>

***чуткий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чуткий.html>чу́ткий</a> (7798)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чуять.html>чу́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čújatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-кий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чуткий.html>чу́ткий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čútkij</span>) (<i>rare/awkward comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)чу́тче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sensitive (of a person, instrument, etc.)</li>
<li>sharp, keen (sense of hearing, smell, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чуткий.html>чу́ткая</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čútkaja</b> sobáka</i> ― <span class="e-translation">keen-nosed dog</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>sympathetic, thoughtful, tactful
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чуткий.html>чу́ткий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:подход.html>подхо́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čútkij</b> podxód</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tactful approach</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>light (sleep)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чуткий.html>чу́ткий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>сон</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čútkij</b> son</i> ― <span class="e-translation">light sleep</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***чуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a> (241)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чуять.html>чу́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čújatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scent, to feel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čutʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a little, slightly
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1982</b>,  Сергей Донатович Довлатов (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sergei_Dovlatov" class="extiw" title="w:Sergei Dovlatov">Sergei Donatovich Dovlatov</a>),  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:зона.html>Зо́на</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:записка.html>Запи́ски</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:надзиратель.html>надзира́теля</a>)</cite> |  translated as Anne Frydman, transl., <cite>The Zone: A Prison Camp Guard's Story</cite>, A.A. Knopf, 1985:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ряд.html>ря́дом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приклеенный.html>прикле́ены</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:фотография.html>фотогра́фии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кинозвезда.html>кинозвёзд</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:журнал.html>журна́ла</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:советский.html>сове́тский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:экран.html>экра́н</a>». <a href = vnd.unilang:кинозвезда.html>Кинозвёзды</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбаться.html>улыба́лись</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:разомкнуть.html>разомкну́в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>гу́бы</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Rjádom býli prikléjeny fotográfii kinozvjózd iz žurnála “Sovétskij ekrán”. Kinozvjózdy ulybálisʹ, <b>čutʹ</b> razomknúv gúby.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Beside these, photographs of film stars from Soviet Screen had been tacked up. The film stars smiled, their lips <b>slightly</b> parted.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>hardly, barely
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1880</b>,  Антон Павлович <a href = vnd.unilang:чех.html>Че́хов</a> (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anton_Chekhov" class="extiw" title="w:Anton Chekhov">Anton Pavlovich Chekhov</a>),  “<a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%97%D0%B0_%D1%8F%D0%B1%D0%BB%D0%BE%D1%87%D0%BA%D0%B8_(%D0%A7%D0%B5%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%B2)" class="extiw" title="s:ru:За яблочки (Чехов)"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>За</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:яблочко.html>я́блочки</a></a>”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Strekoza" class="extiw" title="w:Strekoza"><a href = vnd.unilang:стрекоза.html>Стрекоза́</a></a></cite>  | <cite>Dragonfly</cite> |  |  translated as  “The Little Apples”, in Robert Payne, transl., <cite>The Image of Chekhov: Forty Stories by Anton Chekhov in the Order in Which They Were Written</cite>, A.A. Knopf, 1963, page 8:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:красавица.html>Краса́вица</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:покраснеть.html>покрасне́ла</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слышно.html>слы́шно</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дышать.html>дыша́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прочесть.html>прочла́</a> «<a href = vnd.unilang:отец.html>О́тче</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:наш.html>наш</a>».</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Krasavica pokrasnela i jedva slyšno, <b>čutʹ</b> dyša, pročla “Otče naš”.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The pretty one blushed and recited the Lord's Prayer in a muffled voice, <b>scarcely</b> breathing.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1926</b>,  Михаил Афанасьевич Булгаков (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mikhail_Bulgakov" class="extiw" title="w:Mikhail Bulgakov">Mikhail Afanasyevich Bulgakov</a>),  “<a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9F%D0%BE%D0%BB%D0%BE%D1%82%D0%B5%D0%BD%D1%86%D0%B5_%D1%81_%D0%BF%D0%B5%D1%82%D1%83%D1%85%D0%BE%D0%BC_(%D0%91%D1%83%D0%BB%D0%B3%D0%B0%D0%BA%D0%BE%D0%B2)" class="extiw" title="s:ru:Полотенце с петухом (Булгаков)"><a href = vnd.unilang:полотенце.html>Полоте́нце</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:петух.html>петухо́м</a></a>”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:медицинский.html>Медици́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:работник.html>рабо́тник</a></cite>  | <cite>Medical Worker</cite> |  |  translated as  “The Embroidered Towel”, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Glenny" class="extiw" title="w:Michael Glenny">Michael Glenny</a>, transl., <cite>A Country Doctor's Notebook</cite>, Collins Harvill, 1975, page 21:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тут.html>Тут</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:выйти.html>вы́шел</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:оцепенение.html>оцепене́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взяться.html>взя́лся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пульс.html>пульс</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>В</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:холодный.html>холо́дной</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рука.html>руке́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>Лишь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:после.html>по́сле</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несколько.html>не́скольких</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:секунда.html>секу́нд</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>нашёл</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:заметный.html>заме́тную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:редкий.html>ре́дкую</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:волна.html>волну́</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Tut ja výšel iz ocepenénija i vzjálsja za jejó pulʹs. V xolódnoj ruké jevó ne býlo. Lišʹ pósle néskolʹkix sekúnd našól ja <b>čutʹ</b> zamétnuju rédkuju volnú.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Thereupon I regained my wits and started feeling her pulse. Her cold wrist registered nothing. Only after a few seconds did I detect a <b>barely</b> perceptible, irregular ripple.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слышный.html>слы́шный</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čutʹ</b> slýšnyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>barely</b> audible</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">with <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> almost, nearly
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ли.html>ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:век.html>век</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:назад.html>наза́д</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čutʹ li ne vek nazád</i> ― <span class="e-translation">nearly a century ago</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чуть.html>чуть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:умереть.html>у́мер</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On čutʹ ne úmer.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">He almost died.</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***чучело.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чучело.html>чу́чело</a> (7180)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čučelo</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чучело.html>чу́чело</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čúčelo</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чучело.html>чу́чела</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чучело.html>чу́чела</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чучело.html>чу́чел</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stuffed animal (bird), mount</li>
<li>scarecrow, man of straw, dummy; effigy</li>
<li>scarecrow, fright, bogeyman</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***чушка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чушка.html>чу́шка</a> (24473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">чу́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čúxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чушка.html>чу́шка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čúška</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чушка.html>чу́шки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чушка.html>чу́шки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чушка.html>чу́шк</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">чу́шковый</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> piglet, young pig</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pig's muzzle</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dirty person, especially a child</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal slang<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> schmoe, schmuck <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">dirty, degraded person who anyone can humiliate</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dialectal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> quarter of a pole, for making figures in the game of <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/gorodki" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:gorodki">gorodki</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ingot of metal, usually of cast iron; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">pig iron</i></li></ol>

***чуять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чуять.html>чу́ять</a> (4893)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čùti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)kewh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to perceive</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">show</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">caution</i>, as well as German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">schauen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to look</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, thereby English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">anschauung</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">weltanschauung</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sense of the world, worldview</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чуять.html>чу́ять</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čújatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почуять.html>почу́ять</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:учуять.html>учу́ять</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to smell</li>
<li>to feel, to sense
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нутро.html>нутро́м</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чуять.html>чу́ю</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:добро.html>добру́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja nutróm <b>čúju</b>, ne k dobrú vsjó éto.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have a gut feeling (lit. I <b>feel</b> with [my] inside), this won't mean anything good.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">regional<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hear</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ша.html>ша</a> (16490)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Interjection">Interjection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ша.html>ша</a>!</strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ša!</span>) <i>(uttered in a loud voice)</i>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> shush!, shhh! (be quiet!)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> what!? (<i>surprise, indignation, disgust, excitement or just arrogance</i>) (<i>spoken in Odessa, also in multiple other contexts</i>)</li></ol>

***шабаш.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шабаш.html>шабаш</a> (18022)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">szabas</i> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">שבת</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">shabes</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Sabbath</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">שַׁבָּת</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">shabát</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">subbóta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шабаш.html>ша́баш</a></strong> <i>or</i> <strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шабаш.html>шаба́ш</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šábaš</span> <i>or</i> <span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šabáš</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шабаш.html>ша́баша</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шабаш.html>шаба́ша</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шабаш.html>ша́баши</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шабаш.html>шаба́ши</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шабаш.html>ша́башей</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шабаш.html>шаба́шей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Saturday, observed in Judaism as a day of rest, Sabbath.</li>
<li>A meeting of witches, presided over by the devil, Sabbath.</li>
<li>Any merry debauched festival.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> end of the working day, quitting time (also pronounced šabáš).
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:шабаш.html>Шабаш</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:охотник.html>охо́тники</a>! <a href = vnd.unilang:славный.html>сла́вно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поработать.html>порабо́тали</a>! — <a href = vnd.unilang:веселый.html>ве́село</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:крикнуть.html>кри́кнул</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дедушка.html>де́душка</a>. — <a href = vnd.unilang:сейчас.html>сейча́с</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:пожаловать.html>пожа́луй</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:домой.html>домо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пора.html>пора́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Šabaš</b>, oxótniki! Slávno porabótali! — véselo kríknul déduška. — Sejčás, požáluj, i domój porá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">"That’s it, hunters! We did a great job!" the grandfather shouted merrily. "Now it’s about time we went home."</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Schablone</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">pattern</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***шаг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шаг</a> (368)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шаг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šag</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>ша́га</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шага́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шаги́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шаго́в</a></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* See Usage note.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>step
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шаг</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>ша́гом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">šag za šágom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">step by step</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>pace, stride</li>
<li>démarche</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>After the numbers 2, 3, or 4 when the genitive singular is called for, the stress moves to the case ending: <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:первый.html>пе́рвого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>ша́га</a></span>, <i>but</i> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шага́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>три́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шага́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:сорок.html>со́рок</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:четыре.html>четы́ре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шаг.html>шага́</a></span>.
</p>

***шайка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шайка.html>ша́йка</a> (7222)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ottoman_Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ottoman Turkish language">Ottoman Turkish</a></span> <i class="ota-Arab mention" lang="ota">شایقه</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ota-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">şayka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg"><a href = vnd.unilang:шайка.html>ша́йка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šájka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">saic</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чайка.html>ча́йка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čájka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шайка.html>ша́йка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šájka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шайка.html>ша́йки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шайка.html>ша́йки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шайка.html>ша́ек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> saic, a kind of small boat of up to twelve cannons heavily used in the Black Sea, Tisa, Danube and Sava; similar to the <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ушку́й</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">uškúj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> used in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Republic_of_Novgorod" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Republic of Novgorod">Novgorod</a>
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1769</b>,  <cite>Журналъ военныхъ действій армѣй <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>ея</a> императорскаго <a href = vnd.unilang:величество.html>вели́чества</a></cite>, Saint Petersburg, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.de/books?id=sglQAAAAcAAJamp;pg=PP84amp;dq=%22%D1%88%D0%B0%D0%B9%D0%BA%D0%B8%22v=onepageamp;q=%22%D1%88%D0%B0%D0%B9%D0%BA%D0%B8%22amp;f=false">pages 85–84</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru">Сегожъ <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>числа</a> полученъ рапортъ, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеть.html>хотя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:остальной.html>остальны́е</a> польскіе <a href = vnd.unilang:мятежник.html>мяте́жники</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> которыхъ 10го: <a href = vnd.unilang:число.html>числа</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:упомянутый.html>упомя́нуто</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> разбитіи ихъ <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шайка.html>ша́йки</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:запереться.html>заперши́сь</a> въ замокъ мѣстечка Решова, нѣсколько времяни тамо <a href = vnd.unilang:держаться.html>держа́лись</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> какъ наконецъ <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:недостаток.html>недоста́тку</a> пропитанія <a href = vnd.unilang:принуждённый.html>принуждены́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> оппуда вытти, <a href = vnd.unilang:править.html>правя</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свой</a> путъ <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> мѣстечко Колбушевь, <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дожидавшийся.html>дожида́вшейся</a> ихъ Маіоръ Салеманъ съ <a href = vnd.unilang:команда.html>кома́ндою</a> пустяся немедлѣнно въ слѣдъ <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>ни́ми</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> нагнавъ миляхъ въ <a href = vnd.unilang:семь.html>семи́</a> оть Решова <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a> сихъ мяпeжниковъ въ <a href = vnd.unilang:новь.html>новь</a> атаковалъ, <a href = vnd.unilang:но.html>но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> такимъ образомъ разбилъ, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> мѣстѣ <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> дву сотъ человѣкъ положилъ, <a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a> въ плѣнъ взялѣ тритцатъ человѣкъ съ <a href = vnd.unilang:девять.html>девятью́</a> мѣдными разнаго калибера <a href = vnd.unilang:пушок.html>пушками</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> немалымъ числомъ <a href = vnd.unilang:ружье.html>ру́жей</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> протчей аммуниціи, <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>а</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:начальник.html>нача́льники</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сей.html>сей</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:шайка.html>ша́йки</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:князь.html>Князь</a> Мартынъ Любомнрской <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> нѣкопорой Радзиминскій, способъ <a href = vnd.unilang:найти.html>нашли́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уйти.html>уйти́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́ми</a> полько <a href = vnd.unilang:персона.html>персо́нами</a> въ близь лежащіе лѣса <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> тамо <a href = vnd.unilang:скрыться.html>скры́лись</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Segož čisla polučen raport, što xotja ostalʹnyje polʹskije mjatežniki, o kotoryx 10go: čisla upomjanuto, po razbitii ix <b>šajki</b> zaperšisʹ v zamok městečka Rešova, něskolʹko vremjani tamo deržalisʹ; no kak nakonec po nedostatku propitanija prinuždeny byli oppuda vytti, pravja svoj put na městečko Kolbuševʹ, to dožidavšejsja ix Maior Saleman s komandoju pustjasja nemedlěnno v slěd za nimi i nagnav miljax v semi otʹ Rešova ne tolʹko six mjapežnikov v novʹ atakoval, no i takim obrazom razbil, što na městě do dvu sot čelověk položil, da v plěn vzjalě tritcat čelověk s devjatʹju mědnymi raznago kalibera puškami i nemalym čislom ružej i protčej ammunicii, a načalʹniki sej <b>šajki</b> Knjazʹ Martyn Ljubomnrskoj i někoporoj Radziminskij, sposob našli ujti svoimi polʹko personami v blizʹ ležaščije lěsa i tamo skrylisʹ.</i></dd><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>washtub, tub
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бадья.html>бадья́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">badʹjá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>gang of rogues, band of bandits (originally: sea-raiders on saics, like ushkuiniks)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:банда.html>ба́нда</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bánda</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ватага.html>вата́га</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vatága</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***шалаш.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шалаш.html>шала́ш</a> (10713)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шалаш.html>шала́ш</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šaláš</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шалаш.html>шалаша́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шалаш.html>шалаши́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шалаш.html>шалаше́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>a simple wooden hut</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">criminal  slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the bottom bunk of a bunk bed, with a blanket hanging down from the top bunk as a curtain</li></ol>

***шалить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:шалить.html>шали́ть</a> (17468)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:шалить.html>шали́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">šalítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">пошали́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to play pranks, to be naughty</li>
<li>to play up, to play tricks</li>
<li>to frolic, to romp</li></ol>
